As is so often the case in  China the group of young women on reception duties band together to help the linguistically challenged foreign tourist.

name:W‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçm‚Äçg‚Äçr‚Äça‚Äçy‚Äç8‚Äç1
info:Comfy Double Room
info:Stayed in June 2022
info:Couples
info:47 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 26, 2022
msg:Really nice hotel conveniently located near restaurants and museum. Good place to stay if passing through to Yading, Kaeding, or Chengdu. The hotel has a decent breakfast with a variety of options, all Chinese. 

The hotsprings were closed when I was there due to the government having a meeting the next day. Why they couldn't have them opened made no sense, but it costs extra to utilize them anyway. 

The rooms are equipped with oxygen pumps for 100 RMB a day if you need. The elevation is around 4100 meters so if not acclimatized could be an issue. 

Rooms are modern, very large, and include comfortable beds, large TV with hundreds of channels, for free, but very common in many Chinese hotels. 

Bathrooms are large with separated showers and toilets, as well as sink and mirror. Overall a very quality room with American standard. Highly recommend for a night. 

Great hotpot restaurants nearby and other options.
